<body class="vscode-body vscode-light">
        <h2 id="概述">概述</h2>
<p><mark>FFT可以快速求出两个多项式的乘积/卷积</mark></p>
<p class="katex-block"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mrow><mtable rowspacing="0.1600em" columnalign="center" columnspacing="1em"><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mi>A</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>x</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><msub><mi>a</mi><mn>0</mn></msub><mo>+</mo><msub><mi>a</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mi>x</mi><mo>+</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mo>+</mo><msub><mi>a</mi><mi>n</mi></msub><msup><mi>x</mi><mi>n</mi></msup></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mi>B</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>x</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><msub><mi>b</mi><mn>0</mn></msub><mo>+</mo><msub><mi>b</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mi>x</mi><mo>+</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mo>+</mo><msub><mi>b</mi><mi>n</mi></msub><msup><mi>x</mi><mi>n</mi></msup></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable><mo fence="true">}</mo></mrow><mo>⇒</mo><mtext>求</mtext><mi>A</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>x</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo separator="true">⋅</mo><mi>B</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>x</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\left.\begin{matrix} 
  A(x) = a_0+a_1x+...+a_nx^n \\  
  B(x) = b_0+b_1x+...+b_nx^n \\
\end{matrix}\right\}\Rightarrow  求A(x)·B(x)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:2.40003em;vertical-align:-0.95003em;"></span><span class="minner"><span class="mopen nulldelimiter"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mtable"><span class="col-align-c"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.151392em;"><span style="top:-2.5500000000000003em;margin-left:0em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>这里若使用暴力合并多项式展开为 <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>O</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>+</mo><mn>1</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo separator="true">⋅</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>m</mi><mo>+</mo><mn>1</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">O((n+1)·(m+1))</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.02778em;">O</span><span class="mopen">((</span><span class="mord mathnormal">n</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222222222222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222222222222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mpunct">⋅</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.16666666666666666em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">m</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222222222222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222222222222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mclose">))</span></span></span></span><br>
若使用FFT则是 <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>O</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>n</mi><mi>l</mi><mi>o</mi><mi>g</mi><mi>n</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">O(nlogn)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.02778em;">O</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">n</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.01968em;">l</span><span class="mord mathnormal">o</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.03588em;">g</span><span class="mord mathnormal">n</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></p>
<h2 id="点表示法">点表示法</h2>
<p>任意n+1个不同点均可确定一个n次多项式</p>
<blockquote>
<p class="katex-block"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>x</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>→</mo><msub><mi>x</mi><mrow><mi>n</mi><mo>+</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msub><mo>:</mo><mrow><mo fence="true">{</mo><mtable rowspacing="0.1600em" columnalign="center center center center center center center center center center center center" columnspacing="1em"><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" mathvariant="normal">.</mi></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">+</mo></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" mathvariant="normal">.</mi></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">+</mo></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><msub><mi>a</mi><mi>n</mi></msub><msubsup><mi>x</mi><mrow><mi>n</mi><mo>+</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><mi>n</mi></msubsup></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><msub><mi>y</mi><mrow><mi>n</mi><mo>+</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msub></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">x_1\rightarrow x_{n+1}:
\left\{\begin{matrix}
  &amp;a_0  &amp;+  &amp;a_1x_1  &amp;+  &amp;a_2x_1^2  &amp;+  &amp;...  &amp;+  &amp;a_nx_1^n  &amp;= &amp;y_1 \\
  &amp;a_0  &amp;+  &amp;a_1x_2  &amp;+  &amp;a_2x_2^2  &amp;+  &amp;...  &amp;+  &amp;a_nx_2^n  &amp;= &amp;y_2 \\
  &amp;... \\
  &amp;a_0  &amp;+  &amp;a_1x_n  &amp;+  &amp;a_2x_n^2  &amp;+  &amp;...  &amp;+  &amp;a_nx_n^n  &amp;= &amp;y_n \\
  &amp;a_0  &amp;+  &amp;a_1x_{n+1}  &amp;+  &amp;a_2x_{n+1}^2  &amp;+  &amp;...  &amp;+  &amp;a_nx_{n+1}^n  &amp;= &amp;y_{n+1} 
\end{matrix}\right.</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.58056em;vertical-align:-0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.30110799999999993em;"><span style="top:-2.5500000000000003em;margin-left:0em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing <p>使用了n+1个特殊点</p>
<h3 id="点表示法的好处">点表示法的好处</h3>
<p><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>A</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>x</mi><mo 个点<br>

<h3 id="前提">前提</h3>
<p>系数表示法 <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo><mover><mo><mo>⇌</mo></mo><mtext>快速</mtext></mover></mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\stackrel{快速}{\rightleftharpoons}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1.4603310000000003em;vertical-align:-0.09100000000000001em;"></span><span class="mrel"><span class="mop op-limits"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:1.3693310000000003em;"><span style="top:-2.92em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:3em;"></span><span><span class="mop">⇌</span></span></span><span style="top:-3.7910000000000004em;margin-left:0em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:3em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord cjk_fallback mtight">快速</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.09100000000000001em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> 点表示法</p>
<h3 id="思路流程">思路流程</h3>
<p><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mrow><mtable rowspacing="0.1600em" <h2 id="复数域上的单位根">复数域上的单位根</h2>
<h3 id="复数">复数</h3>
<p><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>a</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>b</mi><mi>i</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a+bi</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.66666em;vertical-align:-0.08333em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">a</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222222222222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222222222222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.69444em;vertical-align:0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">bi</span></span></span></span><br>
<img src="https://img-blog.csdnimg.cn/223ae1ee31c0442abd6f11fe6bb74bc1.png"></p>
<h3 id="运算">运算</h3>
<p>相加： <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>a</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>b</mi><mi>i</mi><mo 相乘： <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>a</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>b</mi><mi>i</mi><mo <h3 id="单位根">单位根</h3>
<img src="https://img-blog.csdnimg.cn/b99ffea1374f4512b9271c2c7ee2c557.png">  
<p>这里用 <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msubsup><mi>ω</mi><mi>n</mi><mi>k</mi></msubsup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\omega_n^k</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1.096108em;vertical-align:-0.247em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.03588em;">ω</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.849108em;"><span style="top:-2.4530000000000003em;margin-left:-0.03588em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">n</span></span></span><span style="top:-3.063em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right:0.03148em;">k</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.247em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> 表示将该单位圆等分为n份，其中的k份被称为n次单位根</p>
<h3 id="性质">性质</h3>
<ol>
<li><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msubsup><mi>ω</mi><mi>n</mi><mi>i</mi></msubsup><mo mathvariant="normal">≠</mo><msubsup><mi>ω</mi><mi>n</mi><mi>j</mi></msubsup><mo separator="true">,</mo><mtext>  </mtext><mi mathvariant="normal">∀</mi><mi>i</mi><mo mathvariant="normal">≠</mo><mi>j</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\omega_n^i\ne \omega_n^j,\;\forall i\ne j</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1.071664em;vertical-align:-0.247em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.03588em;">ω</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.824664em;"><span style="top:-2.4530000000000003em;margin-left:-0.03588em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">n</span></span></span><span style="top:-3.063em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span <h2 id="公式推导">公式推导</h2>
<p><span style="color: red;">正变换：</span> 系数表示法 -&gt; 点表示法<br>
<span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mtable rowspacing="0.2500em" columnalign="right &amp;=(a_0+a_2x^2+...+a_{n-2}x^{n-2})+(a_1x+a_3x^3+...+a_{n-1}x^{n-1})\\

一层一层向下对半拆地递归，分治的思想<br>
<span style="color: red;">逆变换：</span> 点表示法 -&gt; 系数表示法<br>

class="strut" style="height:1.0991079999999998em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.05017em;">B</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right:0.03148em;">k</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" 那么其实本质就是一遍FFT推出点表示，再来一遍推出系数表示<br>
第一遍求 <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>A</mi><mo 第二遍求 <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>B</mi><mo <p><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mtable rowspacing="0.2500em" stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><munderover><mo>∑</mo><mrow><mi>j</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow><mrow><mi>n</mi><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></munderover><msub><mi>a</mi><mi>j</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><munderover><mo>∑</mo><mrow><mi>i</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow><mrow><mi>n</mi><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></munderover><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msubsup><mi>w</mi><mi>n</mi><mrow><mi>j</mi><mo>−</mo><mi>k</mi></mrow></msubsup><msup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mi>i</mi></msup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\begin{aligned}
C_k &amp;= \sum\limits_{i=0}^{n-1}y_k(\omega_n^{-k})^i\\
&amp;=\sum\limits_{i=0}^{n-1}(\sum\limits_{j=0}^{n-1}a_j(\omega_n^i)^j)(\omega_n^{-k})^i\\
&amp;=\sum\limits_{i=0}^{n-1}(\sum\limits_{j=0}^{n-1}a_j(\omega_n^{j-k})^i)\\
&amp;=\sum\limits_{j=0}^{n-1}a_j(\sum\limits_{i=0}^{n-1}(w_n^{j-k})^i)
\end{aligned}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mi>S</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msubsup><mi>ω</mi><mi>n</mi><mi>k</mi></msubsup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mi>S</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>1</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><mi>n</mi></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">S(\omega_n^k):k\left\{\begin{aligned} 
 &amp;\ne0\quad &amp;S(\omega_n^k)&amp;=1+\omega_n^k+\omega_n^{2k}+...+\omega_n^{(n-1)k}\\
 &amp;&amp;\omega_n^k(s(\omega_n^k)&amp;=\omega_n^k+\omega_n^{2k}+...+\omega_n^0\\
&amp;&amp;(1-\omega_n^k)S&amp;=0\\
&amp;&amp;&amp;\because k\ne0时\;\omega_n^k\ne1\quad\therefore S=0\\
&amp;=0\quad &amp;S(\omega_n^k)&amp;=S(1)=n
\end{aligned}\right.</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" <p><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mtable rowspacing="0.2500em" columnalign="right left" columnspacing="0em"><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mspace width="1em"/><mtext>  </mtext><mtext>  </mtext></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><munderover><mo>∑</mo><mrow><mi>n</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow><mrow><mi>n</mi><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></munderover><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>S</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msubsup><mi>ω</mi><mi>n</mi><mrow><mi>j</mi><mo>−</mo><mi>k</mi></mrow></msubsup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\begin{aligned}
\quad\;\;&amp;=\sum\limits_{n=0}^{n-1}(S(\omega_n^{j-k}))
\end{aligned}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:3.3682260000000004em;vertical-align:-1.4341130000000002em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mtable"><span class="col-align-r"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:1.9341130000000002em;"><span style="top:-3.934113em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:3.8011130000000004em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:1em;"></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:1.4341130000000002em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="col-align-l"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span><span class="mop op-limits"><span class="vlist-t mtight">0</span></span></span></span><span style="top:-3.050005em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:3.05em;"></span><span><span class="mop op-symbol large-op">∑</span></span></span><span style="top:-4.300005em;margin-left:0em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:3.05em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">n</span><span class="mbin mtight">−</span><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.03588em;">ω</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.8991079999999998em;"><span style="top:-2.4530000000000003em;margin-left:-0.03588em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing class="vlist" style="height:1.4341130000000002em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<blockquote>
<p>因为只有在 <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>j</mi><mo>=</mo><mi>k</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">j=k</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.85396em;vertical-align:-0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.05724em;">j</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.69444em;vertical-align:0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.03148em;">k</span></span></span></span> 时不得零会被计入后面是n</p>
</blockquote>
<p><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mtable rowspacing="0.2500em" columnalign="right left" columnspacing="0em"><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mo>∴</mo><mtext>  </mtext><mtext>  </mtext><mtext>  </mtext><mtext>  </mtext></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mi>n</mi><msub><mi>a</mi><mi>k</mi></msub></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\begin{aligned}
\therefore\;\;\;\;&amp;=na_k
\end{aligned}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">011</span></span></span></span><span style="top:-3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:3em;"></span><span><span class="mop"><span class="mord underline"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.43056em;"><span style="top:-2.69em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:3em;"></span><span class="underline-line" style="border-bottom-width:0.04em;"></span></span><span style="top:-3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">a</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.30110799999999993em;"><span style="top:-2.5500000000000003em;margin-left:0em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">3</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3499999999999999em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:1.067108em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:1em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mop op-limits"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.43055999999999994em;"><span style="top:-2.032892em;margin-left:0em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:3em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">111</span></span></span></span><span style="top:-3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:3em;"></span><span><span class="mop"><span class="mord underline"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.43056em;"><span style="top:-2.69em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:3em;"></span><span class="underline-line" style="border-bottom-width:0.04em;"></span></span><span style="top:-3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">a</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.30110799999999993em;"><span style="top:-2.5500000000000003em;margin-left:0em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">7</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3499999999999999em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:1.067108em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:2.524388em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><br>
上面的原顺序与递归后的顺序在二进制上是反着的，则反转操作可以是<br>
<code>rev[i]=(rev[i&gt;&gt;1]&gt;&gt;1)|(rev[i]&amp;1)&lt;&lt;(bit-1)</code></p>
<h2 id="程序">程序</h2>
<blockquote>
<p>多项式计算，详情参考<a href="https://www.luogu.com.cn/problem/P3803">LUOGU模板题</a></p>
</blockquote>
<pre><code class="language-cpp"><div><span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">int</span> N = <span class="hljs-number">3000010</span>;
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">double</span> PI = <span class="hljs-built_in">acos</span>(<span class="hljs-number">-1.0</span>);

<span class="hljs-keyword">int</span> n, m;
<span class="hljs-class"><span class="hljs-keyword">struct</span> <span class="hljs-title">Complex</span> {</span> <span class="hljs-comment">// 复数结构体</span>
        <span class="hljs-keyword">double</span> x, y;
        Complex <span class="hljs-keyword">friend</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">operator</span> + ( Complex a, Complex b ) { <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> {a.x + b.x, a.y + b.y}; }
        Complex <span class="hljs-keyword">friend</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">operator</span> - ( Complex a, Complex b ) { <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> {a.x - b.x, a.y - b.y}; }
        Complex <span class="hljs-keyword">friend</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">operator</span> * ( Complex a, Complex b ) { <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> { a.x * b.x - a.y * b.y, a.x * b.y + a.y * b.x}; }
} a[N], b[N]; <span class="hljs-comment">// 两个多项式的点表示</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">int</span> rev[N];   <span class="hljs-comment">// 分治时候的二进制表示对应的结果二进制表示，即反过来了</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">int</span> bit, tot; <span class="hljs-comment">// 二进制上的位数，总个数</span>

<span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">inline</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">void</span> <span class="hljs-title">FFT</span> <span class="hljs-params">( Complex a[], <span class="hljs-keyword">int</span> inv )</span> </span>{
        <span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> ( <span class="hljs-keyword">int</span> i = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>; i &lt; tot; i ++ ) <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> ( i &lt; rev[i] ) swap(a[i], a[rev[i]]); <span class="hljs-comment">// 变成正确的分治结果位置（只能换一半，防止换回来</span>
        <span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> ( <span class="hljs-keyword">int</span> mid = <span class="hljs-number">1</span>; mid &lt; tot; mid &lt;&lt;= <span class="hljs-number">1</span> ) { <span class="hljs-comment">// 枚举分块的块长度</span>
                Complex w1 = {<span class="hljs-built_in">cos</span>(PI / mid), inv * <span class="hljs-built_in">sin</span>(PI / mid)}; <span class="hljs-comment">// 这也是把整个单位圆平均切成mid个后出现的 \omega^1</span>
                <span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> ( <span class="hljs-keyword">int</span> i = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>; i &lt; tot; i += mid * <span class="hljs-number">2</span> ) { <span class="hljs-comment">// 两个两个块向后跳，枚举每一段</span>
                        Complex wk = {<span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>}; <span class="hljs-comment">// w(n, 0)单位一开始</span>
                        <span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> ( <span class="hljs-keyword">int</span> j = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>; j &lt; mid; j ++, wk = wk * w1 ) { <span class="hljs-comment">// 把区间里面数枚举一遍，且wk要往上跑一格</span>
                                Complex x = a[i + j], y = wk * a[i + j + mid]; <span class="hljs-comment">// x把左边提出，y把右边提出</span>
                                a[i + j] = x + y, a[i + j + mid] = x - y;      <span class="hljs-comment">// 左边和右边重构</span>
                        }
                }
        }
}

<span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">int</span> <span class="hljs-title">main</span><span class="hljs-params">()</span> </span>{
        <span class="hljs-built_in">cin</span> &gt;&gt; n &gt;&gt; m;
        <span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> ( <span class="hljs-keyword">int</span> i = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>; i &lt;= n; i ++ ) <span class="hljs-built_in">cin</span> &gt;&gt; a[i].x; <span class="hljs-comment">// 把输入的系数塞入实部</span>
        <span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> ( <span class="hljs-keyword">int</span> i = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>; i &lt;= m; i ++ ) <span class="hljs-built_in">cin</span> &gt;&gt; b[i].x; <span class="hljs-comment">// 把输入的系数塞入虚部</span>
        <span class="hljs-keyword">while</span> ( (<span class="hljs-number">1</span> &lt;&lt; bit) &lt; n + m + <span class="hljs-number">1</span> ) bit ++; <span class="hljs-comment">// 次数最多到n+m+1，所以利用n+m+1记录二进制位数</span>
        tot = <span class="hljs-number">1</span> &lt;&lt; bit; <span class="hljs-comment">// 在二进制位数下计算刚好达不到的那个位数的数</span>
        <span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> ( <span class="hljs-keyword">int</span> i = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>; i &lt; tot; i ++ ) rev[i] = (rev[i &gt;&gt; <span class="hljs-number">1</span>] &gt;&gt; <span class="hljs-number">1</span>) | ((i &amp; <span class="hljs-number">1</span>) &lt;&lt; (bit - <span class="hljs-number">1</span>)); <span class="hljs-comment">// 每个rev[i]初始化为i的二进制逆转</span>
        FFT( a, <span class="hljs-number">1</span> ); FFT( b, <span class="hljs-number">1</span> ); <span class="hljs-comment">// 完成a和b的点表示</span>
        <span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> ( <span class="hljs-keyword">int</span> i = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>; i &lt; tot; i ++ ) a[i] = a[i] * b[i]; <span class="hljs-comment">// 点表示法内完成两方程合并</span>
        FFT( a, <span class="hljs-number">-1</span> ); <span class="hljs-comment">// 逆向做一遍得到系数表示</span>
        <span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> ( <span class="hljs-keyword">int</span> i = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>; i &lt;= n + m; i ++ ) <span class="hljs-built_in">cout</span> &lt;&lt; (<span class="hljs-keyword">int</span>)(a[i].x / tot + <span class="hljs-number">0.5</span>) &lt;&lt; <span class="hljs-string">&quot; &quot;</span>; <span class="hljs-comment">// 防止精度丢失，要向上0.5再强转扔精度</span>
        <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-number">0</span>;
}

</div></code></pre>
    </body>
